## üéÆ HTML5 Game Usage Guide

### Recommended Formats for Web
- **OGG Vorbis** ‚Äî Best for web (smaller, good quality)
- **MP3** ‚Äî Universal fallback
- **WAV** ‚Äî Use only for short SFX (large files!)

### Conversion (WAV ‚Üí OGG)
```bash
# Single file
ffmpeg -i input.wav -c:a libvorbis -q:a 4 output.ogg

# Batch convert all WAV in a folder
find unity-assets/audio/ -name '*.wav' -exec sh -c '
  ffmpeg -i "$1" -c:a libvorbis -q:a 4 "${1%.wav}.ogg"
' _ {} \;
```

### Loading in HTML5 Games
```javascript
// Howler.js (recommended)
const sfx = new Howl({ src: ['sound.ogg', 'sound.mp3'] });
sfx.play();

// Web Audio API
const ctx = new AudioContext();
const response = await fetch('sound.ogg');
const buffer = await ctx.decodeAudioData(await response.arrayBuffer());
```
